(THIS NOTAM IS ONLY FOR CHINA SOUTHERN AIRLINES) 结合一发失效复飞分析结果，A319-115 机型执行ZWTK航线时应遵循以下限制： 1.在签派放行时，15号跑道需要提高着陆标准运行，DA（H）需提高到12420’（1770’），VIS需提高到8000M，即按复飞梯度2.5%的运行标准掌握；33号跑道无特殊要求； 2.在飞行中，机组在执行15 号跑道进近程序时，其复飞决断高需调整为 1770FT，并爬升到13000FT 改平加速收襟翼。 According to Analysis of OEI GA, operation of A319-115 in ZWTK should follow the instructions below, 1.During dispatching flight, the operation standard of RWY15 should be raised so that the DA(H) should be raised to 12420’(1770’) and the VIS to 8000M which means to meet the operation standard of 2.5% GA GRAD.. There is no change to the standard of RWY33. 2.When the flight crew is approaching via RWY15, the DH should be raised to 1770’. Climb to 13000’ to level off and accelerate to retract the flaps when go around.	7
ZBUL AD 2.22飞行程序中增加无线电  通信失效程序 ,具体内容如下 . 5. 无线电通信失效程序  5.1当机组确认通信失效时 ,应立即将应答机编码设置为 7600,并尽可能的尝试与塔台进行联系 . 5.2如航空器具备接收能力 ,应根据接受到的管制指令继续飞行 . 5.3如进港航空器不具备接受能力 ,机组应按照最后接收到的高度指令飞向 HLH并加入标准等待程序进行检查 , 当机组做好落地准备后自行选择进近程序进近 ,到达五边后机组应尽量观察塔台发给的管制灯 光信号以及目视地面信号，根据管制灯光信号决断是 否落地 . 5.4如离港航空器不具备 接收能力 ,应按航空公司要求进行处置 ， 如机组决定继续飞往目的地 ,当塔台能够确认该航空器已飞出本场管制范围后 ,将不再为该 航空器安全负责 .如机组决定返回本场着陆，应按照 5.3执行 ,并保证着陆重量满足要求 . 5.5 灯光信号及目视地面信号按照规章规定执行 ,机组收到灯光信号后 ,按规章规定予以确认 . 5.6如本场不具备落地条件 ,机组应自主决定返航或备降 .	1

(THIS NOTAM IS SPECIAL FOR CHINA SOUTHERN AIRLINES) 根据通告C0539/23，近期北京区域运行的航空器，需进行航空器安全状况通报。 通告C0539/23的正文，以及按正文内容分条校核得到的公司航路 如下所示: 【通告正文：】 C0539/23  NOTAMN  2303030000 -- 2303142359 E)临时安全报告制度的通知：  一 .航空器安全状况通报的时间,范围和报告要求 （一）时间2023年 3月 3日 0时至2023年 3月 14日 23 时 59分 . （二）临时空中限制区范围以天安门为中心半径 150公里划设临时空中限制区 . （三）报告要求 1.以天安门为中心半径 200公里划设安全状态报告圈 .凡去往北京首都机场，北京大兴机场及天津滨海机场落地的航空器，在进入安全状态报告圈前主动向相关管制部门报告航班号（呼号），位置及航空器安全状况.安保报告不正常，或证实安保状态时不予回复的航空器，不得进入 150公里临时空中限制区 . 2.石家庄正定机场，乌兰察布集宁机场，大同云冈机场，张家口宁远机场，承德普宁机场，唐山三女河机场，秦皇岛北戴河机场起飞去往北京首都机场，北京大兴机场及天津滨海机场落地的航空器，当地管制部门须执行起飞前证实安全状况 .即航空器首次联系管制部门时，须由相关管制部门证实航空器安保状况为正常后，方可由发布相关管制放行许可后起飞 . 二 .明确各航路航线飞行时位置报告点 1.沿 W157经 TUMLO 去往北京首都机场，北京大兴机场，天津滨海机场落地的航空器，安全报告位置点为： TUMLO（向北京区管中心报告） 2.沿 W56经 ORODO 去往北京首都机场，天津滨海机场落地的航空器，安全报告位置点为： ORODO（向北京区管中心报告） 3.沿 W62经 ORODO去往北京大兴机场落地的航空器，安全报告位置点为： ORODO（向北京区管中心报告） 4.沿 G212经 TONOV 2.向石家庄正定塔台管制室，乌兰察布集宁机场塔台管制室，大同云冈机场塔台管制室，张家口宁远机场塔台管制室，承德普宁机场塔台管制  室，唐山三女河机场塔台管制室 及秦皇岛北戴河机场塔台管制室报告安保状态的航空器，由相关管制单位按照报告要求进行处置 .安全状态报告不正常的航空器，由负责管制的单位指挥航空器原地等待暂缓移交，并立即向北京区域管制中心进行通报，并根据北京区域管制中心反馈的处置要求执行 . 3.安保报告正常的，管制部门间无需进行通报.安保报告不正常的，管制部门在移交前必须进行特殊通报. 四 .安保报告标准通话用语 P：北  京， XXX101， ...，安保正常 . BEIJING， SECURITY NORMAL,XXX101. 如机组未主动通报安保状况，管制员应主动询问C： XXX101，北京，确认安保状况 . ZNY DE..AIRSPACE WILMINGTON,  DELAWARE..TEMPORARY FLIGHT RESTRICTIONS.        FEBRUARY 24-27, 2023 LOCAL.  PURSUANT TO 49 USC 40103(B)(3), THE FEDERAL AVIATION ADMINISTRATION (FAA) CLASSIFIES THE AIRSPACE DEFINED IN THIS NOTAM AS 'NTL DEFENSE AIRSPACE'. PILOTS WHO DO NOT ADHERE TO THE FOLLOWING PROC MAY BE INTERCEPTED, DETAINED AND INTERVIEWED BY LAW ENFORCEMENT/SECURITY PERSONNEL. ANY OF THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL ACTIONS MAY ALSO BE TAKEN AGAINST A PILOT WHO DOES NOT COMPLY WITH THE RQMNTS OR  ANY SPECIAL INSTRUCTIONS OR PROC ANNOUNCED IN THIS NOTAM: A) THE FAA MAY TAKE ADMINISTRATIVE ACTION, INCLUDING IMPOSING CIVIL PENALTIES AND THE SUSPENSION OR REVOCATION OF AIRMEN CERTIFICATES? OR  B) THE UNITED STATES GOVERNMENT MAY PURSUE CRIMINAL CHARGES, INCLUDING CHARGES UNDER 49 USC SECTION 46307? OR  C) THE UNITED STATES GOVERNMENT MAY USE DEADLY FORCE AGAINST THE AIRBORNE ACFT, IF IT IS DETERMINED THAT THE ACFT POSES AN IMMINENT SECURITY THREAT. EXCEPT AS SPECIFIED BELOW AND/OR UNLESS AUTHORIZED BY ATC IN CONSULTATION WITH THE AIR TRAFFIC SECURITY COORDINATOR VIA THE DOMESTIC EVENTS NETWORK (DEN):   ZNY DE..AIRSPACE WILMINGTON, DELAWARE..TEMPORARY FLIGHT A. ALL AIRCRAFT OPERATIONS WITHIN THE 12 NMR AREA(S) LISTED ABOVE, KNOWN AS THE INNER CORE(S),    ARE PROHIBITED EXCEPT FOR: APPROVED LAW ENFORCEMENT, MILITARY AIRCRAFT DIRECTLY SUPPORTING    THE UNITED STATES SECRET SERVICE (USSS) AND THE OFFICE OF THE PRESIDENT OF THE UNITED STATES,    APPROVED AIR AMBULANCE FLIGHTS, AND REGULARLY SCHEDULED COMMERCIAL PASSENGER AND ALL-CARGO    CARRIERS OPERATING UNDER ONE OF THE FOLLOWING TSA-APPROVED STANDARD SECURITY PROGRAMS/PROCEDURES    AND ARE ARRIVING INTO AND/OR DEPARTING FROM 14 CFR PART 139 AIRPORTS: AIRCRAFT OPERATOR STANDARD    SECURITY PROGRAM (AOSSP), FULL ALL-CARGO AIRCRAFT OPERATOR STANDARD SECURITY PROGRAM (FACAOSSP),    MODEL SECURITY PROGRAM (MSP), TWELVE FIVE STANDARD SECURITY PROGRAM ALL CARGO (TFSSP-ALL CARGO), OR  ALL-CARGO INTERNATIONAL SECURITY PROCEDURE(ACISP). ALL EMERGENCY/LIFE SAVING FLIGHT    (MEDICAL/LAW ENFORCEMENT/FIREFIGHTING) OPERATIONS  MUST COORDINATE WITH ATC PRIOR TO THEIR DEPARTURE    AT 215-492-4123/4185 TO AVOID POTENTIAL DELAYS. B. FOR OPERATIONS WITHIN THE AIRSPACE BETWEEN THE 12 NMR AND 28 NMR AREA(S) LISTED ABOVE, KNOWN AS    THE OUTER RING(S): ALL AIRCRAFT OPERATING WITHIN THE OUTER RING(S) LISTED ABOVE ARE LIMITED TO    AIRCRAFT ARRIVING OR DEPARTING LOCAL AIRFIELDS, AND WORKLOAD PERMITTING, ATC MAY AUTHORIZE TRANSIT    OPERATIONS. AIRCRAFT MAY NOT LOITER. ALL AIRCRAFT MUST BE ON AN ACTIVE IFR OR FILED VFR FLIGHT PLAN    WITH A DISCRETE CODE ASSIGNED BY AN AIR TRAFFIC CONTROL (ATC) FACILITY. AIRCRAFT MUST BE SQUAWKING    THE DISCRETE CODE PRIOR TO DEPARTURE AND AT ALL TIMES WHILE IN THE TFR AND MUST REMAIN IN TWO-WAY    RADIO COMMUNICATIONS WITH ATC. C. ALL FLIGHT OPERATIONS NOT COVERED IN PARAGRAPH A. WITHIN THE 12 NMR AREA MUST BE SECURITYSCREENED BY  TSA AT A GATEWAY AIRPORT PRIOR TO ARRIVING OR DEPARTING NEW CASTLE AIRPORT (KILG) .    AIRCRAFT OPERATORS MUST REGISTER WITH THE TSA FOR GATEWAY SCREENING NO LESS THAN 24 HOURS PRIOR TO    THEIR SCHEDULED DEPARTURE TIME. RESERVATIONS FOR SCREENING MAY BEGIN ON 02/23/2023 AND LAST THROUGH    THE DURATION OF THE EVENT BY CALLING TSA AT 610-537-9027. D. GATEWAY AIRPORTS HAVE BEEN CREATED AT NEW CASTLE AIRPORT (KILG) , ALLENTOWN INTERNATIONAL    AIRPORT (KABE) AND DULLES INTERNATIONAL AIRPORT（KIAD) BY TSA TO ACCOMMODATE AIRCRAFT ARRIVING OR    DEPARTING NEW CASTLE AIRPORT (KILG). E. TSA SCREENING WILL NOT BE AVAILABLE ON FRIDAY, 02/24/2023. TSA SCREENING WILL BE AVAILABLE    EFFECTIVE 2302251300 UTC (0800 LOCAL 02/25/23) TO 2302252200 UTC (1700 LOCAL 02/25/23). TSA    SCREENING WILL BE AVAILABLE 2302261300 UTC (0800 LOCAL 02/26/23) TO 2302262200 UTC (1700 LOCAL    02/26/23). TSA SCREENING WILL NOT BE AVAILABLE ON MONDAY, 02/27/2023. PILOTS, CREW AND PASSENGERS    MUST PROVIDE VALID GOVERNMENT-ISSUED PHOTO IDENTIFICATION TO THE TSA AT THE GATEWAY AIRPORT.    GATEWAY SCREENING WILL INCLUDE ID VERIFICATION AND VETTING OF ALL PILOTS, CREW AND PASSENGERS,    SCREENING OF PERSONS AND BAGGAGE, AND INSPECTION OF THE AIRCRAFT. NO FIREARMS ON BOARD AIRCRAFT WILL BE AUTHORIZED. NO GIFT WRAPPED PACKAGES. F. ON DEPARTURE FROM A GATEWAY AIRPORT AIRCRAFT MUST MAINTAIN RADIO CONTACT WITH ATC AND    CONTINUOUSLY SQUAWK AN ATC-ASSIGNED DISCRETE CODE. INTERMEDIATE STOPS WHILE ENROUTE ARE NOT AUTHORIZED UNLESS AN EMERGENCY EXISTS. G. THE FOLLOWING OPERATIONS ARE NOT AUTHORIZED WITHIN THIS TFR: FLIGHT TRAINING, PRACTICE    INSTRUMENT APPROACHES, AEROBATIC FLIGHT, GLIDER OPERATIONS, PARACHUTE OPERATIONS, ULTRALIGHT, HANG    GLIDING, BALLOON OPERATIONS, AGRICULTURE/CROP DUSTING, ANIMAL POPULATION CONTROL FLIGHT    OPERATIONS, BANNER TOWING OPERATIONS, SIGHTSEEING OPERATIONS, MAINTENANCE TEST FLIGHTS, MODEL AIRCRAFT OPERATIONS, MODEL ROCKETRY, UNMANNED    AIRCRAFT SYSTEMS (UAS), AND UTILITY AND PIPELINE    SURVEY OPERATIONS. H. UAS OPERATORS WHO DO NOT COMPLY WITH APPLICABLE AIRSPACE RESTRICTIONS ARE WARNED THAT PURSUANT TO    10 U.S.C. SECTION 130I AND 6 U.S.C. SECTION 124N,    THE DEPARTMENT OF DEFENSE (DOD) , THE DEPARTMENT OF HOMELAND SECURITY (DHS) OR THE DEPARTMENT OF    JUSTICE (DOJ) MAY TAKE SECURITY ACTION THAT   RESULTS IN THE INTERFERENCE, DISRUPTION, SEIZURE,    DAMAGING, OR DESTRUCTION OF UNMANNED AIRCRAFT DEEMED TO POSE A CREDIBLE SAFETY OR SECURITY    THREAT TO PROTECTED PERSONNEL, FACILITIES, OR ASSETS. I. THE SYSTEM OPERATIONS SUPPORT CENTER (SOSC), IS THE COORDINATION FACILITY FOR GOVERNMENT AGENCIES    AND IS AVAILABLE DAILY FROM 0700-2300 EASTERN,PHONE 202-267-8276 FOR COORDINATION. J.
